<html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="explosion_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">explosion<span class="pron">(kspl<span class="underline">o</span><sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for explosion" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/197/19778/19778.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">explosions</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for explosion" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/197/19779/19779.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="explosion_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>explosion</strong> is a sudden, violent burst of energy, for example one caused by a bomb.</span><span class="orth"><q>  After the second explosion, all of London's main train and subway stations were shut
                  down.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Three people have been killed in a bomb explosion in northwest Spain.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="explosion_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Explosion</strong> is the act of deliberately causing a bomb or similar device to explode.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Bomb disposal experts blew up the bag in a controlled explosion.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="explosion_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>explosion</strong> is a large rapid increase in the number or amount of something.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">in</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The study also forecast an explosion in the diet soft-drink market.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The spread of the suburbs has triggered a population explosion among America's deer.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="explosion_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>explosion</strong> is a sudden violent expression of someone's feelings, especially anger.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Every time they met, Myra anticipated an explosion.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="explosion_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>explosion</strong> is a sudden and serious political protest or violence.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the explosion of protest and violence sparked off by the killing of seven workers.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h3>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Spice up</strong> means the same as  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="spice#spice_1">spice</a></span></span>.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> <span class="smallcaps">P</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Her publisher wants her to spice up her stories with sex.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n <span class="smallcaps">P</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...a discovery which spiced the conversation up quite a bit.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">

    <a id="incidentally_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">incidentally<span class="pron">(<span class="underline"></span>nsd<span class="underline">e</span>ntli<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for incidentally" data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/280/28066/28066.mp3"></a>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="incidentally_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. adverb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>incidentally</strong> to introduce a point which is not directly relevant to what you are saying, often
               a question or extra information that you have just thought of.</span><span class="orth"><q>  'I didn't ask you to come. Incidentally, why have you come?'</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="incidentally_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adverb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something occurs only <strong>incidentally</strong>, it is less important than another thing or is not a major part of it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The letter mentioned my great-aunt and uncle only incidentally.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing is <strong>incidental</strong> to another, it is less important than the other thing or is not a major part of it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The playing of music proved to be incidental to the main business of the evening.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="quarter_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. fraction</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>quarter</strong> is one of four equal parts of something.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  A quarter of the residents are over 55 years old.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I've got to go in a quarter of an hour.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Prices have fallen by a quarter since January.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Cut the peppers into quarters.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Quarter</strong> is also a predeterminer.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The largest asteroid is Ceres, which is about a quarter the size of the moon.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Quarter</strong> is also an adjective.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the past quarter century.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>quarter</strong> is a fixed period of three months. Companies often divide their financial year into
               four quarters.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The group said results for the third quarter are due on October 29.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you are telling the time, you use <strong>quarter</strong> to talk about the fifteen minutes before or after an hour. For example, 8.15 is <strong>quarter past</strong> eight, and 8.45 is <strong>quarter to</strong> nine. In American English, you can also say that 8.15 is a <strong>quarter after</strong> eight and 8.45 is a <strong>quarter of</strong> nine.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It was a quarter to six.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I got a call at quarter of seven one night.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>quarter</strong> something such as a fruit or a vegetable, you cut it into four roughly equal parts.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Chop the mushrooms and quarter the tomatoes.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.15" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If the number or size of something <strong>is quartered</strong>, it is reduced to about a quarter of its previous number or size.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The doses I suggested for adults could be halved or quartered.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.17" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>quarter</strong> is an American or Canadian coin that is worth 25 cents.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I dropped a quarter into the slot of the pay phone.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.19" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A particular <strong>quarter</strong> of a town is a part of the town where a particular group of people traditionally
               live or work.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Look for hotels in the French Quarter.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.21" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To refer to a person or group you may not want to name, you can talk about the reactions
               or actions from a particular <strong>quarter</strong>.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Help came from an unexpected quarter.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.23" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">9. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The rooms provided for soldiers, sailors, or servants to live in are called their
               <strong>quarters</strong>.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Mckinnon went down from deck to the officers' quarters.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="quarter_1.25" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">10. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you do something <strong>at close quarters</strong>, you do it very near to a particular person or thing.</span><span class="orth"><q>  You can watch aircraft take off or land at close quarters.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

The verb that follows <strong>politics</strong> may be either singular or plural.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The key question in British politics was how long the prime minister could survive.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The film takes no position on the politics of Northern Ireland.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Politics is by no means the only arena in which women are excelling.</q></span></li>
      </ol>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Your <strong>politics</strong> are your beliefs about how a country ought to be governed.</span><span class="orth"><q>  My politics are well to the left of centre.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="politics_1.8" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Politics</strong> is the study of the ways in which countries are governed.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He began studying politics and medieval history.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...young politics graduates.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="politics_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Politics</strong> can be used to talk about the ways that power is shared in an organization and the
               ways it is affected by personal relationships between people who work together. The
               verb that follows <strong>politics</strong> may be either singular or plural.</span><span class="orth"><q>  You need to understand how office politics influence the working environment.</q></span></li>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>prime</strong> to describe something that is of the best possible quality.</span><span class="orth"><q>  It was one of the City's prime sites, near the Stock Exchange.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prime_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>prime</strong> to describe an example of a particular kind of thing that is absolutely typical.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The prime example is Macy's, once the undisputed king of California retailers.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prime_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone or something is <strong>in</strong> their <strong>prime</strong>, they are at the stage in their existence when they are at their strongest, most
               active, or most successful.</span><span class="orth"><q>  She was in her intellectual prime.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  We've had a series of athletes trying to come back well past their prime.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...young persons in the prime of life.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prime_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>prime</strong> someone <strong>to</strong> do something, you prepare them to do it, for example by giving them information about
               it beforehand.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Claire wished she'd primed Sarah beforehand.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Arnold primed her for her duties.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed to-inf]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The press corps was primed to leap to the defense of the fired officials.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prime_1.17" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="pump#pump_1">prime the pump</a></span></span></div>
</div></div>

   <div id="accept_1.1" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>accept</strong> something that you have been offered, you say yes to it or agree to take it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Eventually Sam persuaded her to accept an offer of marriage.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  All those invited to next week's peace conference have accepted.</q></span></li>

      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="accept_1.11" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>accept</strong> an unpleasant fact or situation, you get used to it or recognize that it is necessary
               or cannot be changed.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  People will accept suffering that can be shown to lead to a greater good.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Urban dwellers often accept noise as part of city life.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> that]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I wasn't willing to accept that her leaving was a possibility.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="accept_1.15" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If a person, company, or organization <strong>accepts</strong> something such as a document, they recognize that it is genuine, correct, or satisfactory
               and agree to consider it or handle it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  We advised newspapers not to accept the advertising.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Cheques can only be accepted up to the value guaranteed on the card.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n  <em class="hi">as</em> n/adj]</span></li>

   </div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If an organization or person <strong>accepts</strong> you, you are allowed to join the organization or use the services that are offered.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  All-male groups will not be accepted.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...incentives to private landlords to accept young people as tenants.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n  <em class="hi">into</em> n]</span></li>

               you do.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  My grandparents have never had a problem accepting me.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Many men still have difficulty accepting a woman as a business partner.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">into</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Stephen Smith was accepted into the family like an adopted brother.</q></span></li>

   <div id="implication_1.1" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>implications</strong> <strong>of</strong> something are the things that are likely to happen as a result.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The Attorney General was aware of the political implications of his decision to prosecute.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The low level of current investment has serious implications for future economic growth.</q></span></li>

   <div id="implication_1.4" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>implication</strong> of a statement, event, or situation is what it implies or suggests is the case.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The implication was obvious: vote for us or it will be very embarrassing for you.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
      <div id="implication_1.6" class="hom">
         <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">phrase</span> 
         </h4>
         <ol class="sense_list level_0">
            <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that something is the case <strong>by implication</strong>, you mean that a statement, event, or situation implies that it is the case.</span><span class="orth"><q>  His authority and, by implication, that of his management team is under threat.</q></span></li>
         </ol>
      </div>

</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">exercises</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for exercise" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/195/19556/19556.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">exercising</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for exercise" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/195/19557/19557.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">exercised</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for exercise" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/195/19555/19555.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="exercise_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>exercise</strong> something such as your authority, your rights, or a good quality, you use it or put
               it into effect.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  They are merely exercising their right to free speech.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Britain has warned travellers to exercise prudence and care.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exercise</strong> is also a noun.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the exercise of political and economic power.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Leadership does not rest on the exercise of force alone.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you <strong>exercise</strong>, you move your body energetically in order to get fit and to remain healthy.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  She exercises two or three times a week.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Exercising the body does a great deal to improve one's health.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exercise</strong> is also a noun.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Lack of exercise can lead to feelings of depression and exhaustion.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If a movement or activity <strong>exercises</strong> a part of your body, it keeps it strong, healthy, or in good condition.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  They call rowing the perfect sport. It exercises every major muscle group.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.12" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exercises</strong> are a series of movements or actions which you do in order to get fit, remain healthy,
               or practise for a particular physical activity.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I do special neck and shoulder exercises.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exercises</strong> are military activities and operations which are not part of a real war, but which
               allow the armed forces to practise for a real war.</span><span class="orth"><q>  General Powell predicted that in the future it might even be possible to stage joint
                  military exercises.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>exercise</strong> is a short activity or piece of work that you do, for example in school, which is
               designed to help you learn a particular skill.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Try working through the opening exercises in this chapter.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.18" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you describe an activity as an <strong>exercise</strong> <strong>in</strong> a particular quality or result, you mean that it has that quality or result, especially
               when it was not intended to have it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">in</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  As an exercise in stating the obvious, this could scarcely be faulted.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Think what a waste of taxpayers' money the whole exercise was.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exercise_1.21" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>exercises</strong> you or your mind, you think or talk about it a great deal, especially because you
               are worried or concerned about it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  This has been a major problem exercising the minds of scientists around the world.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing is <strong>opposite</strong> another, it is on the other side of a space from it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Jennie had sat opposite her at breakfast.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Opposite</strong> is also an adverb.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He looked up at the buildings opposite, but could see no open window.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="opposite_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>

      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="opposite_1.6" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Opposite</strong> is used to describe things of the same kind which are completely different in a particular
               way. For example, north and south are opposite directions, and winning and losing
               are opposite results in a game.</span><span class="orth"><q>  All the cars driving in the opposite direction had their headlights on.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  I should have written the notes in the opposite order.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>opposite</strong> <strong>of</strong> someone or something is the person or thing that is most different from them.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Ritter was a very complex man but Marius was the opposite, a simple farmer.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Well, whatever he says you can bet he's thinking the opposite.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you <strong>ride</strong> a horse, you sit on it and control its movements.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I saw a girl riding a horse.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Can you ride?</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He was riding on his horse looking for the castle.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> adv/prep]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  They still ride around on horses.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you <strong>ride</strong> a bicycle or a motorcycle, you sit on it, control it, and travel along on it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Riding a bike is great exercise.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Two men riding on motorcycles opened fire on him.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> prep/adv]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He rode to work on a bicycle.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you <strong>ride</strong> <strong>in</strong> a vehicle such as a car, you travel in it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">in/on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He prefers travelling on the Tube to riding in a limousine.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> adv/prep]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I remember the village full of American servicemen riding around in jeeps.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>ride</strong> is a journey on a horse or bicycle, or in a vehicle.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Would you like to go for a ride?</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.15" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In a fairground, a <strong>ride</strong> is a large machine that people ride on for fun.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that one thing <strong>is riding on</strong> another, you mean that the first thing depends on the second thing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Billions of pounds are riding on the outcome of the election.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.18" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="lbl">see also</span> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="riding#riding_1">riding</a></span></span></div>
   <div id="ride_1.19" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that someone or something <strong>is riding high</strong>, you mean that they are popular or successful at the present time.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He was riding high in the public opinion polls.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.21" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">9. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that someone faces <strong>a rough ride</strong>, you mean that things are going to be difficult for them because people will criticize
               them a lot or treat them badly.</span> (<span class="lbl register">informal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  The Chancellor could face a rough ride unless the plan works.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.23" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">10. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that someone <strong>has been taken for a ride</strong>, you mean that they have been deceived or cheated.</span> (<span class="lbl register">informal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  When he had not returned with my money an hour later I realized that I had been taken
                  for a ride.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ride_1.25" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="roughshod#roughshod_1">to ride roughshod over</a></span></span></div>
</div>
<div class="re hom-subsec">
   <ul class="sense_list level_1">
      <li> <span class="xr"> See  <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="ride-out#ride-out_1">ride out</a></span></span></li>
      <li> <span class="xr"> See  <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="ride-up#ride-up_1">ride up</a></span></span></li>
   </ul>
</div></div>

<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="compound_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">compound</h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">compounds</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">compounding</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for compound" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/110/11045/11045.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">compounded</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for compound" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/110/11044/11044.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div class="semantic">The noun is pronounced <span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>mpand<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/636/63654/63654.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>. The verb is pronounced <span class="pron">(kmp<span class="underline">a</span>nd<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/636/63656/63656.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>.
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>compound</strong> is an enclosed area of land that is used for a particular purpose.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Police fired on them as they fled into the embassy compound.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a military compound.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In chemistry, a <strong>compound</strong> is a substance that consists of two or more elements.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Organic compounds contain carbon in their molecules.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is a <strong>compound</strong> <strong>of</strong> different things, it consists of those things.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Honey is basically a compound of water, two types of sugar, vitamins and enzymes.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Compound</strong> is used to indicate that something consists of two or more parts or things.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a tall shrub with shiny compound leaves.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the compound microscope.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In grammar, a <strong>compound</strong> noun, adjective, or verb is one that is made up of two or more words, for example
               'fire engine', 'bottle-green', and 'force-feed'.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.12" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In grammar, a <strong>compound</strong> sentence is one that is made up of two or more main clauses. Compare  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="complex#complex_1">complex</a></span></span>.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>compound</strong> a problem, difficulty, or mistake means to make it worse by adding to it.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Additional bloodshed and loss of life will only compound the tragedy.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">by</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The problem is compounded by the medical system here.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If snow <strong>drifts</strong>, it builds up into piles as a result of the movement of the wind.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The snow, except where it drifted, was only calf-deep.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="drift_1.17" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>drift</strong> is a mass of snow that has built up into a pile as a result of the movement of wind.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a nine-foot snow drift.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="drift_1.19" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">9. singular noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>drift of</strong> an argument or speech is the general point that is being made in it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Grace was beginning to get his drift.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div>
<div class="re hom-subsec">
   <ul class="sense_list level_1">
      <li> <span class="xr"> See  <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="drift-off#drift-off_1">drift off</a></span></span></li>
   </ul>
</div></div>

</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">triumphed</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for triumph" data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/581/58184/58184.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="triumph_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>triumph</strong> is a great success or achievement, often one that has been gained with a lot of skill
               or effort.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The championships proved to be a personal triumph for the coach, Dave Donovan.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Cataract operations are a triumph of modern surgery, with a success rate of more than
                  90 percent.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="triumph_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Triumph</strong> is a feeling of great satisfaction and pride resulting from a success or victory.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Her sense of triumph was short-lived.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="triumph_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone or something <strong>triumphs</strong>, they gain complete success, control, or victory, often after a long or difficult
               struggle.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  All her life, Kelly had stuck with difficult tasks and challenges, and triumphed.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">over</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The whole world looked to her as a symbol of good triumphing over evil.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

    <a id="ration_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">ration<span class="pron">(r<span class="underline"></span><sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for ration" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/443/44323/44323.mp3"></a>

<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">rations</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for ration" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/443/44340/44340.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">rationing</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for ration" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/443/44339/44339.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">rationed</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for ration" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/443/44338/44338.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="ration_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When there is not enough of something, your <strong>ration</strong> of it is the amount that you are allowed to have.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The meat ration was down to one pound per person per week.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ration_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When something <strong>is rationed</strong> by a person or government, you are only allowed to have a limited amount of it, usually
               because there is not enough of it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Staples such as bread, rice and tea are already being rationed.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the decision to ration food.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Motorists will be rationed to thirty litres of petrol a month.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ration_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Rations</strong> are the food which is given to people who do not have enough food or to soldiers.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Aid officials said that the first emergency food rations of wheat and oil were handed
                  out here last month.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ration_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Your <strong>ration</strong> <strong>of</strong> something is the amount of it that you normally have.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...after consuming his ration of junk food and two cigarettes.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="ration_1.11" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="lbl">see also</span> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="rationing#rationing_1">rationing</a></span></span></div>
</div></div>

      </h3>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can refer to a place where a particular group of people lives as a particular
               kind of <strong>colony</strong>.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a penal colony.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...industrial colonies.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="colony_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>colony</strong> <strong>of</strong> birds, insects, or animals is a group of them that live together.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The Shetlands are famed for their colonies of sea birds.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="except_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. preposition</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>except</strong> to introduce the only thing or person that a statement does not apply to, or a fact
               that prevents a statement from being completely true.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I wouldn't have accepted anything except a job in Europe.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  I don't take any drugs whatsoever, except aspirin for colds.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Except</strong> is also a conjunction.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Freddie would tell me nothing about what he was writing, except that it was to be
                  a Christmas play.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="except_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>except for</strong> to introduce the only thing or person that prevents a statement from being completely
               true.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He hadn't eaten a thing except for one forkful of salad.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Everyone was late, except for Richard.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

    <a id="prejudice_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">prejudice<span class="pron">(pr<span class="underline">e</span>dds<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for prejudice" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/420/42039/42039.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">prejudices</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for prejudice" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/420/42041/42041.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">prejudicing</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for prejudice" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/420/42043/42043.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">prejudiced</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for prejudice" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/420/42040/42040.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="prejudice_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Prejudice</strong> is an unreasonable dislike of a particular group of people or things, or a preference
               for one group of people or things over another.</span><span class="orth"><q>  There is widespread prejudice against workers over 45.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  He said he hoped the Swiss authorities would investigate the case thoroughly and without
                  prejudice.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prejudice_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>prejudice</strong> someone or something, you influence them so that they are unfair in some way.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I think your South American youth has prejudiced you.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>  <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He claimed his case would be prejudiced if it became known he was refusing to answer
                  questions.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prejudice_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>prejudices</strong> another person's situation, they do something which makes it worse than it should
               be.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Her study was not in any way intended to prejudice the future development of the college.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="prejudice_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you take an action <strong>without prejudice to</strong> an existing situation, your action does not change or harm that situation.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  We accept the outcome of the inquiry, without prejudice to the unsettled question
                  of territorial waters.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

   <div id="relic_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you refer to something or someone as a <strong>relic</strong> <strong>of</strong> an earlier period, you mean that they belonged to that period but have survived into
               the present.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Germany's asylum law is a relic of an era in European history which has passed.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="relic_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>relic</strong> is something which was made or used a long time ago and which is kept for its historical
               significance.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a museum of war relics.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>rsum</strong> is a short account, either spoken or written, of something that has happened or that
               someone has said or written.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I will leave with you a resum of his most recent speech.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Your <strong>rsum</strong> is a brief account of your personal details, your education, and the jobs you have
               had. You are often asked to send a rsum when you are applying for a job.</span> (<span class="lbl geo">mainly US</span>)
            <div class="semantic">in BRIT, usually use <strong>curriculum vitae</strong></div>
         </li>
      </ol>
